We successfully refunded the 50,000 yuan we were defrauded of. The hotel is our home in a foreign land, which gives us a sense of security. msg:The mountains are high and the road is far away, look at the world and find yourself.
It was the first time in my life that I entered Tibet and stayed at the InterContinental Hotel on the first night in Lhasa. That night, the altitude sickness was very severe. I felt dizzy, had a headache, felt hot all over my body, felt cold and had diarrhea. I called the staff in the morning, the lobby manager Zhang Lulu found out and immediately sent a delicious breakfast to replenish my energy. After packing up and going downstairs, Zhang Lulu took me to inhale medical oxygen for half an hour. Seeing that I was weak, he gave me 2 bottles of oxygen to take with me Carry it, so that I can take a car to Nyingchi for a smooth trip. When I came back to Lhasa two days later, when I checked in at the front desk, I met Zhang Lulu who was full of smiles. When I learned that I would stay for 3 nights, she immediately upgraded me to a business room with a view of the quiet garden inside. The warm feeling of being at home washed away my exhaustion from plateau and travel. The big business room gave me the comfort of my home, and I thank Lulu for giving me the warmth and touch of my trip to Tibet alone! After staying for 3 nights, I asked Lulu to register and stayed for another night. Before the opening of the 5th Tibet Tourism and Culture International Expo, I left the warm hotel like home. Thank you Lulu for making my trip to Tibet full of wonderful memories! Next time I come to Lhasa again, I hope to find Lulu to check in at the InterContinental Hotel.
Because of the particularity of Lhasa's high altitude, I hope that the hotel has more excellent staff who can bring more warmth and touch to guests who have serious high-altitude reactions.
